<strong>Welcome to the the best shots groups!</strong>  Thanks for posting your picture to the first level of our group. If your picture receives 4 awards, you can post it to <a href="/groups/1508184@N20/" rel="nofollow">the best shots Level 2</a> If your picture receives at least 2 awards, you can <a href="/groups/1529824@N23/discuss/72157625044014238//" rel="nofollow">post it here</a>, to receive more awards. <strong>Please dont forget, that you have to award at least 5 other pictures!</strong>  <a href="http://www.flickr.com/groups/1529824@N23"><img src="http://farm5.static.flickr.com/4132/4992787333_4cac235f96_m.jpg" width="160" height="160" /> </a>  <strong>Have fun - Your admin and moderator team!</strong>
